DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV MAVEN_HOME=/opt/maven
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$MAVEN_HOME/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3-pip \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash
  # Initialize SDKMAN! and install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal)
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk use java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalPython component
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Install Apache Maven latest stable (download and install official binary)
  RUN MAVEN_VERSION=3.9.4 && \
      wget https://dlcdn.apache.org/maven/maven-3/${MAVEN_VERSION}/binaries/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION}-bin.tar.gz -O /tmp/maven.tar.gz && \
      tar xf /tmp/maven.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION} $MAVEN_HOME && \
      rm /tmp/maven.tar.gz
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists and set ownership to root
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV MAVEN_HOME=/opt/maven
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$MAVEN_HOME/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3-pip \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash
  # Initialize SDKMAN! and install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal)
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk use java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalPython component
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Install Apache Maven latest stable (download and install official binary)
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      MAVEN_VERSION=3.9.4 && \
      wget https://dlcdn.apache.org/maven/maven-3/${MAVEN_VERSION}/binaries/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION}-bin.tar.gz -O /tmp/maven.tar.gz && \
      tar xf /tmp/maven.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION} $MAVEN_HOME && \
      rm /tmp/maven.tar.gz
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python -m venv /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists and set ownership to root
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV MAVEN_HOME=/opt/maven
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$MAVEN_HOME/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3-pip \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash
  # Initialize SDKMAN! and install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal)
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk use java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalPython component
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Install Apache Maven latest stable (download and install official binary)
  RUN mkdir -p /opt; \
      MAVEN_VERSION=3.9.4; \
      wget https://dlcdn.apache.org/maven/maven-3/${MAVEN_VERSION}/binaries/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION}-bin.tar.gz -O /tmp/maven.tar.gz && \
      tar xf /tmp/maven.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION} /opt/maven && \
      rm /tmp/maven.tar.gz
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python -m venv /gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists and set ownership to root
  RUN mkdir -p /gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV MAVEN_HOME=/opt/maven
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$MAVEN_HOME/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3-pip \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash
  # Initialize SDKMAN! and install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal)
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk use java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalPython component
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Install Apache Maven latest stable (download and install official binary)
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      MAVEN_VERSION=3.9.4 && \
      wget --tries=5 --timeout=30 https://dlcdn.apache.org/maven/maven-3/${MAVEN_VERSION}/binaries/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION}-bin.tar.gz -O /tmp/maven.tar.gz && \
      tar xf /tmp/maven.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION} /opt/maven && \
      rm /tmp/maven.tar.gz
  # Verify Maven installation
  RUN /opt/maven/bin/mvn -version
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python -m venv /gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists
  RUN mkdir -p /gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV MAVEN_HOME=/opt/maven
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$MAVEN_HOME/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3-pip \
      wget \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash
  # Initialize SDKMAN! and install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal)
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk use java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalPython component
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Install Apache Maven latest stable (download and install official binary)
  RUN mkdir -p /opt && \
      MAVEN_VERSION=3.9.4 && \
      wget --tries=5 --timeout=30 --no-check-certificate https://downloads.apache.org/maven/maven-3/${MAVEN_VERSION}/binaries/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION}-bin.tar.gz -O /tmp/maven.tar.gz && \
      tar xf /tmp/maven.tar.gz -C /opt && \
      ln -s /opt/apache-maven-${MAVEN_VERSION} /opt/maven && \
      rm /tmp/maven.tar.gz
  # Verify Maven installation
  RUN /opt/maven/bin/mvn -version
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python -m venv /gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists
  RUN mkdir -p /gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 5 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8
  ENV LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/root/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/root/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV MAVEN_HOME=/opt/maven
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$MAVEN_HOME/bin:$PATH
  WORKDIR /gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3-pip \
      wget \
      maven \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install SDKMAN!
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash
  # Initialize SDKMAN! and install GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal)
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && \
      sdk use java 17.0.7-graal"
  # Install GraalPython component
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && \
      $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Verify Maven installation
  RUN mvn -version
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python -m venv /gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists
  RUN mkdir -p /gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 6 ---

  WORKDIR /gluetest
  # Install prerequisites
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      unzip \
      zip \
      tar \
      git \
      bash \
      ca-certificates \
      python3.11 \
      python3.11-venv \
      python3.11-distutils \
      wget \
      maven \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install pip for python3.11 explicitly
  RUN wget https://bootstrap.pypa.io/get-pip.py -O /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      python3.11 /tmp/get-pip.py && \
      rm /tmp/get-pip.py
  # Install SDKMAN! and GraalVM Java 17 (17.0.7-graal) in one step
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 17.0.7-graal && sdk use java 17.0.7-graal" 
  # Install GraalPython component with proper environment
  RUN bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && $JAVA_HOME/bin/gu install python"
  # Verify Maven installation
  RUN mvn -version
  # Create python3 alias and upgrade pip, install pytest globally using python3.11 explicitly
  RUN ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.11 /usr/bin/python && \
      python3.11 -m pip install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel && \
      python3.11 -m pip install pytest
  # Set up Python virtual environment in project root
  RUN python3.11 -m venv /gluetest/venv
  # Update .bashrc to add GraalVM, Maven, JAVA_HOME and activate python venv on shell start
  RUN echo "export SDKMAN_DIR=$SDKMAN_DIR" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export JAVA_HOME=$JAVA_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export MAVEN_HOME=$MAVEN_HOME" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "export PATH=\$JAVA_HOME/bin:\$MAVEN_HOME/bin:\$PATH" >> /root/.bashrc && \
      echo "source /gluetest/venv/bin/activate" >> /root/.bashrc
  # Ensure working directory exists
  RUN mkdir -p /gluetest
  # Set default shell to bash and start at working directory
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 7 ---
